British Air Force Budget Submitted to the House of Commons, An Additional £3,000,000, Totaling £23,851,000, MacDonald Announces New Invention of Air Defense Law

(London) Air Force Undersecretary Sir Sassoon submitted the Air Force budget for 1935 to the House of Commons today, stipulating an additional expenditure of £3,089,000, with a total net expenditure for the year of £20,650,000, and a gross amount of £23,851,000, an increase of £3,685,000 compared with 1934. Sir declared that for the sake of peace, the US government has delayed implementing Britain's lowest air defense procedures in the past decade. The weakness of Britain's air defense is a danger to world peace and Britain itself. Britain can no longer allow its air force to rank fifth in the first line of strength among air powers. At the same time, he did not want to exaggerate the weakness of the British Air Force. At present, only the first line of strength in France and Russia is far superior to Britain. The number of aircraft in the United States and Italy is only slightly better than that of Britain, but there are fewer qualified pilots in active service than in the Royal Air Force. The design and performance of the Royal Air Force's aircraft are not inferior to any country, but technical progress has been very rapid in recent years, so in addition to increasing the number of aircraft, it is also necessary to re-determine the equipment procedures. He hopes that the construction period of new aircraft can be shortened in the future. The British aircraft manufacturing industry can still make profits. The total value of British aircraft exports in 1934 increased by 31% compared with 1933. There are currently 29 foreign countries using British aircraft and 33 foreign countries using British aviation engines. At the same time, the expansion of the Royal Air Force has had to first increase the number of air stations and airfields. The additional expenditure of 3.5 million pounds in the 1934 budget was mostly due to this project. The Air Force is now offering a reward of £25,000 to British manufacturers to produce the best commercial aircraft. It is also planned to manufacture two high-altitude and long-range experimental aircraft. If they are satisfactory, Britain intends to win the world record for altitude and non-stop flight.

One of the highlights of the debate was the remarks made by Mr. Churchill. According to reports, the actual strength of the British and German air vehicles was equal in November last year. Since then, Britain's position has been worse. Today, Germany has at least 6 days of first-line aircraft, and there is a possibility of increasing it to about 1,500 in 1935-36. Britain's air force program is extremely inadequate and has entered a very dangerous period. The great war that ended in 1918 may be repeated today, but he still hopes and believes that it can be saved in the end. Sir Sassoon replied that according to the latest news received by the government, there are various reasons to believe that the British Air Force is still stronger than Germany today.

Since October last year, the overall situation has deteriorated to a certain extent, and the manufacture of German aircraft has been greatly accelerated, but he believes that Britain can still have a slight advantage by the end of this year. Britain's program is defensive and can be increased or decreased at any time according to the needs of the situation.

The hope of limiting armaments has not been abandoned. He does not think that accelerating expansion has now reached the final necessity, but the overall situation is very worrying today. The government will not slacken in the full protection of the country and the entire empire. The Air Force budget stipulates that by the end of 1938, the Royal Air Force will increase by a total of four and a half detachments, and stipulates that the first-line strength will have a total of 1,330 aircraft, plus 120 aircraft in the irregular team. The National Defense Force will increase by 11 new detachments, totaling 54 detachments, of which 41 detachments are for regular duty, and the rest are auxiliary or special reserves. The Air Force of the Navy Fleet will increase by 11 first-line aircraft. This new organization will increase the strength of the British Air Force, including the aircraft of the fleet, to a total of 105 and a half detachments. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(London) British Prime Minister MacDonald briefly described the British government's plan for the defense against sky attacks in the House of Commons today, saying that the government is not satisfied with relying solely on counterattacks to protect the sky. A committee of scientific experts was organized months ago to investigate the possibility of using the latest inventions to resist sky attacks. The committee has prepared concrete proposals and has now started preliminary tests. The government decided to appoint a special committee on sky defense to unify the work of the navy and civil affairs in the field of sky defense. This special committee will conduct a full investigation and raise the necessary funds for research. (19th Reuters Telegram)

German Military Aircraft Appear Publicly for the First Time, Large-Scale Air Defense Exercises in Berlin

(Berlin) German Air Force exercises began tonight. First, 40 military aircraft flew in Beijing and its suburbs for a long time. Since the European War, today is the first time that military aircraft have flown over the capital. Residents are very interested in the air defense exercises. In the evening, all the houses in the city had their lights turned off and their windows closed. All kinds of vehicles driving on the streets had their lights covered. People were stationed on the bell towers of various churches to monitor whether residents were complying with the order to turn off the lights. At 11 o'clock, it was assumed that enemy air forces came to bomb, and the city would be completely dark at that time. (20th Havas Telegram)

(Berlin) This afternoon, 36 newly established air force fighter planes and 15 bombers held their first exercises in the sky over the city. Residents all craned their necks to watch and were very interested. At one point, the planes flew in close formation, skimming over the rooftops, causing the crowd to feel anxious. The Commander-in-Chief of the Air Force, Aviation General Göring, ordered the team to come here. His intention was clearly to show the public the horror of aerial warfare. At the same time, Foreign Minister Neurath told a Reuters reporter that the measures Germany is taking now are necessary for equality, and Head of State Hitler has announced that he will never use this new army and air force for aggression, so the general feeling of security should be made a reality. Mr. Niu also said that if Europe has another great war, Europe will come to an end. The discussions after British Foreign Secretary Simon comes here will not be easy, but the current basis is clearer than before. (19th Reuters Telegram)

(Berlin) Berlin became a dark world from 10 p.m. to midnight tonight, because at that time, soldiers and civilians were practicing large-scale air defense exercises. At exactly 10 o'clock, the lights in all store windows were turned off, and the windows of all homes, cafes, restaurants, and factories were covered with black cloth, so that no light leaked out. At exactly 11 o'clock, most of the street lights were also turned off. The remaining 1,500 street lights were also covered with thick black cloth, leaving only a small circle of round light below. As a result, the entire city was as dark as a dead city. This afternoon, a team of 24 fighter planes and several bombers soared into the sky to inform the residents of Berlin of the preparations for tonight's exercises in advance. (19th National Telegram)

(Berlin) Air defense exercises were held last night, assuming that enemy air forces would bomb the capital at 11 o'clock, and ordered all residents of the city to implement fire control at that time, and promulgated defense measures, assigning personnel to guard the houses everywhere to monitor the implementation. The exercises were successfully completed at midnight. Residents were very satisfied with the execution of the orders. (20th Havas Telegram)

Russia Trains 140,000 Youths as Air Force Reserves, Borli Commemorates No-Takeoff Aviation Festival

(Moscow) The Central Committee of the Soviet Russian Youth League and the Aviation Committee have agreed that 140,000 young people from agricultural fields will be gathered this year to be trained as aviation pilots, and 30,000 young women will be trained for Red Cross rescue work. In addition, farmers will be encouraged in various ways to make them feel interested in aviation. The Soviet Russian military authorities have approved the organization of 1,100 aviation teaching institutes this year to train farmers to become air force reserves. It is said that the government has raised funds to cover this expense. (20th National Telegram)

Borli: Here to celebrate the Soviet Far East Aviation Memorial Day, aviator Ivanov is famous for flying on the Far East aviation route between Borli and Huaye Island. He has flown 300,000 kilometers. He has been flying on this route for 1,500 hours. In the past three years, Ivanov has never encountered any danger or accidents. (19th TASS Telegram)

Japan Lends 33 Million Yuan to the Puppet State, Payment Due at Signing of the Sino-Eastern Railway

(Tokyo) Among the 180 million yuan of public bonds issued by "Manchukuo" to acquire the Sino-Eastern Railway, the first payment of 30 million yuan was originally scheduled for April 6. After Committee Chairman Tomii reported on the review process of the Review Committee, the original proposal was approved unanimously. (20th Japan United Telegram)

Current Commentary

A Perspective on England's Note of Protest to Germany

— Wei

Since Germany recently declared the establishment of an air force and the implementation of compulsory military service, the only country in Europe that has been alarmed is not France. France is particularly alarmed. For the past fifteen years after the war, France has regarded England as its right and left hand in diplomacy. Therefore, England participated in the Locarno Pact, the Paris Convention, the Lausanne Agreement, and the London Agreement. In the London Agreement, England and France intended to replace the military clauses of Part V of the Treaty of Versailles with "general military measures." France granted Germany the right to military equality, and England mediated to enable Germany to return to Geneva to discuss disarmament. This was already a very big concession for France, but Germany still felt it was not enough. Therefore, the London Agreement was still fresh, and Germany announced the establishment of an air force and rearmament.

Germany's expansion of armaments is to ensure its own security and must have active countermeasures. England, with the London Agreement in place, cannot stay out of the matter. Will England uphold its commitment to promoting the law to suppress Germany, or will it abandon its promise and promote Germany to suppress France? One of the two must be the case. Judging from the content of England's note of protest to Germany, England's attitude seems difficult to grasp. At first, it said, "After the German government announced the air force, it had the latest declaration, which, in addition to the point of principle in dispute, greatly increased the unrest in Europe." Then it said, "England has concentrated its efforts in Geneva to seek the success of replacing the military clauses of Part V of the Treaty of Versailles with general military measures." From the former, it seems to support France's past position, while from the latter, it seems to support Germany's actions today. There should be no support for the latter if there is criticism of the former, and there should be no criticism of the former if there is support for the latter. With England's diplomatic tact, there should be no such contradiction. There must be a deep meaning in this. Generally speaking, from the perspective of European international relations, France is only afraid of Germany, while England is only afraid of Russia. It is not afraid of Germany. France fears German revenge, and Russia fears German aggression. The targets of France and Russia are the same, so the two countries have the possibility of uniting. However, Germany has ambitions to invade Russian territory, and England has a national policy of preventing Russia from instigating rebellions in its colonies. Their targets are also the same. The union of England and Germany is also not impossible. On the day Germany announced its rearmament, the English Foreign Secretary's visit to Berlin did not stop. Its purpose was not so much to "enhance universal understanding" as it was to win over Germany to form an anti-Russian bloc.

If the above analysis is not far from the truth, then the division of military and diplomatic affairs in Europe in the future is very obvious. In order to defend against German revenge and eastern aggression, France and Russia will form a large group, and the Little Entente will be its wings. In order to rectify the military, promote militarism, and prevent the expansion of red forces, Germany and England can also form a group, and Poland and Japan will be its wings. Today's military alliance diplomacy is very similar to the situation on the eve of the Great War in 1914. Who says that the current situation of international peace in Europe is not in imminent danger?

朝日 Plane Flies to Beijing

(Nanjing) The "Asahi Plane," for the Sino-Japanese goodwill flight of the Tokyo and Osaka Asahi Shimbun companies, which departed from Tokyo's Haneda Airport at 7:46 this morning, covering a new air route of 2,500 kilometers, appeared in the sky over Nanjing from the Jinpu Railway direction at 5:30 PM. After circling around, it landed at Ming Palace Airport at 5:38 PM amidst cheers. Consul General Suma and other Japanese residents in Beijing, as well as representatives from various Chinese circles, had been waiting at the airport to welcome them. Upon seeing the plane, they waved flags and cheered. After pilot Shinya and engineer Tsukagoshi disembarked, they underwent customs inspection. Representatives from the Japanese elementary school in Nanjing presented them with flowers, and a toast was held in the newly established picnic area at the airport. After a welcoming speech by representatives of the Nanjing press, the two heroes retired to their lodgings. At 7 PM, they attended a welcoming banquet hosted by Consul General Suma at the consulate, and representatives from various Chinese circles were also invited. Furthermore, at 9 AM on the 21st, the two heroes paid their respects at Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum and presented wreaths. Then, they visited various Chinese institutions. At noon on the 22nd, they departed from Beijing for Shanghai. (20th, Dentsu News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Asahi Shimbun's plane visiting the capital safely arrived in Nanjing at 5:30 PM this afternoon. (20th, Japan United Press dispatch)

Jiangsu Provincial Government Stipulates Methods for Physical Training of Civil Servants

(Zhenjiang) The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in order to comply with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's (2nd) telegram and promote the physical training of civil servants, has stipulated that every civil servant, except those with physical disabilities or those over 50 years of age who may freely choose to participate, must select one of the following: Chinese martial arts, fitness, equestrianism, archery, apparatus exercises, track and field, basketball, football, tennis, volleyball, and other ball sports. Practice sessions will be held daily from 5:00 PM to 6:00 PM, or from 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM in winter, and this will be considered part of their performance evaluation. The management committees have already been organized by various agencies and will be implemented soon. (20th, Central News Agency dispatch)

After touring Tiantai tomorrow morning, they will return to Hangzhou on the 22nd. (20th, Special dispatch)

Beijing Military Police Department Captures Culprit Who Stole Long-Distance Telephone Wires

(Nanjing) The Jinghu (Beijing-Shanghai) long-distance telephone lines in Qilinmen, Maqun Town, and other places have been stolen more than 14 times since last summer. Each time they were cut, Beijing-Shanghai telephone communication was immediately interrupted. Although repairs were made promptly, the time and economic losses were significant. Although rewards were offered for the arrest of the thief, the wire theft continued to occur. On the 18th of this month, the Criminal Investigation Team of the Military Police Department saw a person coming from Maqun, carrying two large bundles of purple copper wires. They immediately arrested him and found an insulated wire cutter and a steel file. He confessed to stealing the wires and said that Lou Yushan was the mastermind. On the morning of the 19th, Lou was also arrested. He confessed that he was formerly a squad leader in the Revenue Police Corps of the Ministry of Finance. He also revealed accomplices Zhi Yixi and Han Jinzhao, who were also arrested. Fifty-seven catties of wire were recovered. The entire case has now been handed over to the Garrison Headquarters for legal action. (20th, Special dispatch)

Ministry of Communications to Abolish Long-Distance Telephone Management Offices in Various Provinces

(Nanjing) In order to unify the management of long-distance telephone and wired telegraph services in various provinces, the Ministry of Communications has ordered the long-distance telephone management offices in Jiangsu, Shandong, Anhui, Hebei, Henan, and other provinces to be abolished, effective April 1st. A long-distance telephone administrator will be established within the Bureau of Telecommunications Administration of each province, and the original administrator of the long-distance telephone management office will be appointed to that position. (20th, Special dispatch)

Governor-General and Wife of French West Africa Die, Five Companions Also Die

(Paris) French West African Governor-General Renard, his wife, three military officers, a pilot, and a radio operator went missing several days ago while inspecting the Lake Chad area by plane. It has now been ascertained that the plane crashed 150 kilometers south of Haut-Uele, Belgian Congo. All seven people on board were killed. Renard was formerly the Prefect of the Seine Department. In February of last year, he resigned at the same time as the Paris Police Commissioner Chiappe due to the Stavisky affair. His wife, the daughter of an American millionaire, also died tragically. In addition, the five military officers, pilot, and radio operator did not survive. It is also said that Renard's son died in a flying accident several years ago. (19th, Havas News Agency dispatch)

Brussels It was reported that the Governor-General of French Equatorial Africa, Mr. and Mrs. Rinar, and others went missing last Friday on an inspection tour by plane, and it was later reported that they had landed safely in a certain place in the Belgian Congo, with everyone on board unharmed. However, according to an official who arrived here today, Mr. and Mrs. Rinar and five companions were killed in the plane crash, and the fuselage was broken into pieces. According to the circumstances, the plane must have flown into a sandstorm, causing the pilot to lose control and make an emergency landing, resulting in this disaster due to excessive force upon landing. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

Conflict Between Indian Muslims and Military Police, 27 Dead, 97 Wounded

Karachi This morning, there was a conflict between Muslim protesters and military police. The military police fired 47 shots, killing 27 protesters and wounding 97. Although the city appears to be peaceful on the surface, people are still quite agitated. Troops are stationed at key points to prevent further incidents. Indian officials said that the authorities took swift and decisive action this time, preserving thousands of Indian women and children. A resident with a great reputation said that the British soldiers' actions saved the city from disaster. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

After Resignation of Belgian Cabinet, All Parties Still Support Gold Standard, but France Believes Belgium Will Join Sterling Bloc, and Says Netherlands Will Take Similar Action

Brussels After the resignation of the cabinet, the general impression is that a unified national cabinet should be organized, and it should be announced that the current exchange rate of the Belgian franc will be maintained. Socialist leader Vandervelde recently met with the King and, upon leaving the palace, stated that he had discussed with the King whether to dissolve the parliament and hold general elections. (19th, Havas News Agency dispatch)

Brussels Belgian Prime Minister Theunis declared in the House of Representatives today that the opposition party's movement against the government's plan to protect the Belgian currency was the cause of the cabinet's resignation. The government has been fighting for the Belgian currency since February 4, but the opposition party's movement prevented it from stopping the harm suffered by the Belgian franc. Before resigning, the government had taken the necessary measures to protect the national currency. He hopes that the new cabinet will receive the unified assistance of the entire country to overcome the future crisis. After Theunis's resignation, the right wing of the House of Representatives held a meeting and decided to support the policy of maintaining the gold standard, with only two votes against. At the same time, the left wing of the Senate also passed a similar resolution. The Socialist Party also declared its support for maintaining the gold standard. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

(Paris) People here believe that the resignation of the Belgian cabinet was due to the French government's decision not to lend 4 billion francs to Belgium and not to give it sufficient commercial concessions. It is widely believed that Belgium will join the Sterling bloc, and the Netherlands seems to be taking similar action. It is expected that President Hoover will have an unexpected opportunity to submit the holding of a currency conference to the world. All gold standard countries now have a sense of panic. This afternoon, France formally provided assistance to the Belgian currency. It seems that France's hope of helping Belgium has not completely disappeared. After the resignation of the Belgian cabinet, the immediate impact on the London market was a rapid increase in the exchange rate of the pound sterling, due to a large demand for the pound sterling from Europe. However, the London stock market was uneasy because it feared that commercial competition would become more intense after Belgium abandoned the gold standard. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

(New York) The foreign exchange market was very chaotic today after the Belgian cabinet collapsed. Gold coins, when converted into US dollars, were initially strong, but then plummeted, and the market atmosphere at the close was very panicky. The stock market did not seem to be affected by this. There were no major increases or decreases in Belgian securities. However, the closing price of the Belgian 7% public bond due in 1935 was 108.125, a decrease of 5.875 compared to Monday. People here regard the Belgian government's establishment of an exchange control bureau as a transitional measure, and it is possible that a more far-reaching plan will be formulated soon, or that all gold coins will be devalued uniformly. Some quarters believe that the sale of a large amount of raw cotton by foreign countries, especially France, shows that they want to obtain more US dollars in order to offset the losses that will be caused by the future devaluation or abandonment of the gold standard by the franc. Judging from this situation, speculators do not have much confidence in the ability of gold standard countries to maintain the gold standard, which can be seen generally. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

The Hague The Dutch government today submitted a bill stipulating a reduction of £8.5 million in government expenses, the purpose of which is to transfer these saved funds to a fund for protecting the Dutch currency. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

Italy and Abyssinia Refuse to Concede to Each Other in Dispute, New Incident Occurs in North Africa

(Rome) The Italian government today proposed to the Abyssinian government that the border dispute be resolved by the ambassadors of the two countries, without resorting to the Italo-Abyssinian Conciliation Commission. Negotiations between the two countries to resolve the dispute broke down a few days ago, so Abyssinia invoked Article 15 of the League of Nations Covenant and petitioned the League of Nations. At the same time, both sides are still trying their best to salvage what appears to be a dangerous situation. A message was received here today from Italian Somaliland stating that a dispute had occurred on the border, but the details are not yet known. (20th, Reuters dispatch)

(Rome) A new incident has occurred on the border between Abyssinia and Italian Somaliland. In the area near Akobo, Abyssinia, an armed force robbed more than 100 camels between the Ernat and Korogoaya stations. Italian patrol soldiers immediately rushed to the area to pursue them, but the armed force had already retreated into Abyssinian-controlled territory. The Italian soldiers stopped at the border and did not pursue them further, to avoid causing further incidents. The Italian embassy in Abyssinia has received instructions from the government to formally protest to the Abyssinian government about this matter, and reserves the right to demand compensation for the losses suffered by Italian citizens. (20th, Havas News Agency dispatch)

(Rome) The Italian authorities issued a declaration today denying everything, because Abyssinia has repeatedly used foreign newspapers to launch attacks against Italy. According to the Italian statement, first, Italy has never rejected the proposal made by Abyssinia to organize an arbitration committee; second, the statement that Italy has ignored all documents delivered by Abyssinia is meaningless; third, the Italian government's dispatch of troops to Somaliland and Eritrea is of a self-defense nature and has not been secret, and the air force personnel accompanying the army to Africa are no more than what is applied in the ratio of troops sent to Africa. Finally, according to repeated reports from consuls, Abyssinia has recently mobilized troops to Somaliland, and this mobilization order has recently extended to the northern part of Abyssinia. According to reliable sources, the Italian government has sent a reply to the Abyssinian capital regarding the proposal to organize an arbitration committee. According to its contents, Italy believes that the possibility of a direct solution has not yet disappeared, and in order to quickly resolve all existing difficulties, direct negotiations are the only way. Italy is not opposed to arbitration, but only feels that the method of arbitration is too slow and complicated. Therefore, Italy has put forward a counter-proposal, which should involve the exchange and detailed examination of documents related to the various tragedies, along with the causes before the tragedies and the results after the tragedies, by the Abyssinian Foreign Minister and the Italian Ambassador to Abyssinia, so that the true situation can be revealed. The opinions put forward by Italy are also those proposed by the League of Nations, and are the fastest, most practical, and most effective solutions. (19th, National News Agency dispatch)

(Geneva) The document that Abyssinia sent to the Secretariat of the League of Nations, requesting the Council of the League of Nations to impartially mediate the dispute between Abyssinia and Italy in accordance with Article 15 of the League of Nations Charter, has been published here today. The document states that the dispatch of troops to Africa by Italy has created a dangerous situation of rupture between Abyssinia and Italy, and that in accordance with the methods proposed by the League of Nations General Assembly on January 19, Abyssinia and Italy should immediately begin direct negotiations, in order to quickly resolve the disputes caused by the incidents of mid-December last year. However, so far, Italy has neither shown a significant tendency to agree to direct negotiations, nor is willing to accept the mediation of a third party proposed by Abyssinia, and Italy has not expressed any opinion on Abyssinia's request to submit this case to arbitration, but has instead dispatched troops to Africa as a reply. The document also mentions Article 10 of the League of Nations Charter, which states that all member states of the League of Nations should respect each other's territorial integrity. The document further declares that Abyssinia is willing to maintain friendly relations with Italy, but for the sake of its rights and interests, it may request mediation in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of the Charter. The document does not request the Council of the League of Nations to convene an immediate meeting, so the League of Nations will probably not deal with it drastically, but will wait for the next meeting of the Council in May. (19th, National News Agency dispatch)

Germany Releases Arrested Clergy

(Berlin) On Saturday night, Nazi authorities arrested more than a hundred clergymen in Berlin and elsewhere to prevent them from reading proclamations against Archbishop Mueller on Sunday. Now that the goal has been achieved, all the people have been released today. (19th, Reuters dispatch)

Gold and Silver

London Gold Price Because the pound sterling was strong when the price was quoted, the price today was 145 shillings and 6 pence, 1 shilling and 8.5 pence lower than yesterday. The London silver market continued to fall today. The spot price is 27 pence 125, and the futures price is 27 pence 1875, both down 1875. India and China sold, and the United States bought. Supply exceeded demand, so the price was low and weak.

Exchange Rates

US-UK In the London foreign exchange market, the opening exchange rate between the US and the UK was 4 yuan 7 jiao 8 fen, 375 lower than the closing price of the US and UK yesterday. Then, due to good demand, the price rose again. At 10:45, it rose 2 fen to 4 yuan 8 jiao. Soon the market became calm, but there were still people buying pounds sterling, so at 11 o'clock it rose another 125. Then, due to a temporary lull in buying, the price fell 2 fen to 4 yuan 7 jiao 8 fen 125. At 12 o'clock, there were a few buyers, and the price stabilized again, rising 125. However, at 1 o'clock in the afternoon, it fell 625 to 4 yuan 7 jiao 7 fen 625. The market then turned firm again, rising 875 at 2 o'clock to 4 yuan 7 jiao 8 fen half, a net increase of half a fen compared to this morning's opening.

UK-France The opening price was 72 francs 43, 28 pounds lower than yesterday's closing price. It rose and fell repeatedly, and at 2 pm the price was 72 francs 65, 22 pounds higher than the opening price.

US-UK New York Foreign Exchange The market was unstable. The opening exchange rate against the British pound was 4 yuan 7 jiao 8 fen half, 125 lower than yesterday's closing price.

US-France The opening exchange rate against the French franc in New York was 6 yuan 5 jiao 9 fen half, unchanged.

Cotton and Wheat

US Cotton Before the opening of the New York cotton market this morning, it was predicted that the market atmosphere would be panicked and prices would fall. However, when the market opened, the price actually rose 6 pounds higher than yesterday's closing price. Within ten minutes, foreign sales rose again, and the price fell back to the same level as yesterday's closing price. The bulls also made some settlements, which was also the reason for the price decline. The market was inactive, but there was an uneasy atmosphere in the market, which was enough to limit buying and selling. Later, there was new buying, and the price rose slightly, but trading was still not active.

US Wheat Although there were reports of cloudy and rainy weather in the wheat area in the Chicago wheat market, the price rose slightly at the opening today, expressing sympathy for foreign telegrams. The price in Winnipeg also rose slightly.

UK Wheat The market sentiment was better in the Liverpool wheat market today. At 1:00 PM, the price for the May period was 5 shillings and 75, 625 higher than yesterday's closing price.

Cotton The Liverpool cotton market was quieter, and the industry paid little attention. At 1:00 PM, the price for the May period was 6.05, 1 pound lower than yesterday's closing price.

Rubber

London The rubber market was sluggish today, and the industry and speculators did not show much interest. At noon, the transaction price for the July-September period was 5 pence 625, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York The futures market opened in the rubber market today, up about 2 pounds. The market was still stable, due to good foreign telegrams. Trading was quiet and few transactions were made.

Securities

New York Due to the unrest in the European situation, trading was restricted. Interest was very low when the securities market opened, but the market price was still . It was heard that there was a slight increase.

Mussolini's Eastern Policy and the Great Organization Under It (Correspondence from Rome)

Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has been in power for thirteen years. While focusing on internal affairs, he has recently strived to expand the nation's power abroad. In Europe, he initially sympathized with Germany, jointly calling for the revision of the Treaty of Versailles. Subsequently, he allied with France, gaining partial sovereignty in Africa. He employed both diplomatic and military means to the best of his ability. In recent years, he has apparently adopted a "conciliatory policy" towards Eastern Asia. While the purpose of this policy is not something we can know, our country is clearly one of its targets. Therefore, we must pay close attention to its organizational activities. Here is an account of the two major Eastern organizations newly established in Rome:

(1) The Institute for Oriental Studies

The Institute for Oriental Studies (Istituto Italiano Per il Medio ed Estremo Oriente) is an Italian academic organization dedicated to the study of Eastern issues. It is located at No. 61 Via Monte Serrato, Rome. The president is Qin Dilai, a current member of the Senate. Mr. Qin Dilai is quite wealthy and extremely enthusiastic about Eastern studies. The institute was inaugurated at the same time as the First Oriental Students' Association and has been in operation for over a year. (For details on the opening of the Oriental Students' Association, see last year's Shen Bao Monthly). The institute's organizational structure, in addition to the president, includes a vice president and a secretary. Members include many individuals with considerable political or social standing and those with a strong interest in Eastern issues. The institute places particular emphasis on the Far East and has established Chinese and Japanese language study classes. Teachers are hired to teach in the same classroom, but at different times. The institute also has a reference room. The reporter once visited and observed a considerable collection of Chinese and Japanese books and newspaper materials. The newspaper clippings are classified on cards, and each room contains bookshelves filled with publications on Eastern issues.

Mussolini once gave a public lecture at the institute. On average, such public lectures are held once a week. On the 12th of this month, Hua Lai, the former Italian Minister to China, gave a lecture on "The Dawn of a New Chinese Culture." A large audience attended, including Liu Wendao, our ambassador to Italy. Although his remarks contained some distortions of the situation in China (he was stationed in China in 1928, and much of what he said related to the situation several years ago), his attitude was fair, and he expressed great sympathy for China and praised the New Life Movement. On the 18th of this month, Father Buliya was specially invited to lecture on the life of Mr. Sun Yat-sen and his influence on the Chinese nation.

The institute also publishes many books on Eastern issues, all printed in Italian and sold at the institute and in bookstores. After each lecture, the speech is usually sent to newspapers in Rome and elsewhere.

(2) The Oriental Students' Association

The Confederation of Oriented Students has also been established for more than a year and has held two general assemblies. The first was in December of the year before last, which Mussolini himself attended. More than a hundred Chinese students from various European countries came to Rome, along with about six hundred students from other Eastern countries, making it a grand occasion. After the meeting, the Oriental Students' Association was officially established, and it was resolved to establish a permanent office in Rome.

The second assembly was held from December 27th to 31st of last year. Representatives from Chinese students studying in Germany, Austria, and Italy, the Indian and Ceylon European Students' Association, Siamese students studying in France, Belgium, the Netherlands, and Germany, Arab students studying in Switzerland and France, Egyptian students studying in Germany and France, Japanese students studying in Switzerland, and Javanese students studying in Germany attended, totaling about 150 people. The meeting resolved to draft new organizational regulations to revise the content of the Oriental Students' Association. Previously, the association consisted entirely of individual members. The new general regulations changed it into an alliance of student organizations. It was also decided that the association would be divided into three organizations: "General Assembly," "Board of Directors," and "Standing Committee." During the subsequent election of officers, there was a brief dispute because Japanese representative OGHISSIMA, a student studying in Switzerland, colluded with Persian representative Hossein Danesch, a student studying in Germany, to sabotage the association. They first advocated for the re-election of the incumbent president as the president of this session because Danesch was the first president. However, their plan was opposed by the majority. Therefore, the general assembly resolved to express a vote of no confidence in the former president, passing the motion by a vote of 120 to 16 to elect a new president. Danesh then withdrew from the assembly, and Egyptian representative Galal, the former vice president, also resigned. The assembly ignored this and elected Liao Jiabao, the Chinese representative, as president, and Indian representative Sundaram, B. Litt, and Arab representative Chekil el-Djabri as vice presidents. One representative each from Siam, Annam, Ceylon, and China served as honorary secretaries and accountants. The four members of the Standing Committee were Indian representatives Saxker and Dubash, Arab representative Salem, and Chinese representative Lin Jiesheng. Before the election was completed, the Egyptian representative suddenly expressed his intention to withdraw his resignation, but because the matter had already been announced, the assembly did not consider it further.

Therefore, China can be said to have had a considerable victory in the second assembly. The failure of the Japanese representative's conspiracy further stabilized the foundation of the Oriental Students' Association. On January 16th of this year, the association issued a notice to all parties, stating that the association's purpose was to "promote the cultural and general interests of Eastern students studying in Europe" and solemnly stated that "all elections and discussions in the association are based on the free will of the students and are not influenced by external forces. At the same time, Eastern students studying in Europe are welcome to provide more assistance so that it can become a completely independent cultural organization." The attitude is open and aboveboard, and there is nothing to criticize. However, it is unknown whether the facts will be as stated. The association publishes a publication called "New Asia," with its address at No. 1 Via Del Cobservatorio. (February 18th)

Inspection Tour of the Northwest

— Special Correspondent Geng Ya

A Glimpse of the Life of the Chantu People in Xinjiang

The Chantu people account for approximately 60% or more of the total population of Xinjiang. Their language, script, appearance, and customs are all different from those of other ethnic groups. They have high noses, deep-set eyes, and sturdy builds, resembling Westerners. However, their skin is brownish-yellow, their eyes and hair are black, and they traditionally wear beards, shaved in an arc from the ears to the lower jaw, in what is called the "ten-ear style." Approximately 1,300 years ago, Islam, "holding the scriptures in one hand and the sword in the other," conquered eastwards over the Pamir Mountains, capturing Kashgar and other places. The Chantu people came under their rule and unanimously converted to Islam. Their script is written horizontally from right to left, with twenty-two letters, including fifteen vowels and seventeen consonants. The pronunciation is light and smooth, with many guttural and lingual sounds and few labial and dental sounds, sharing a common origin with Turkish, although there are slight differences in intonation. The language is consistent, for example, calling father "Dadan," mother "Alang," children "Balangzi," girls "Keqi," and boys "Wokeluo," etc. Those who engage in public business or trade learn to speak Chinese out of necessity, but the pronunciation is difficult to articulate clearly. For example, one popular ditty they like to sing originally says, "I'd rather eat plain glory than scallions, I'd rather be a commoner than a soldier. Alas, alas, those who eat the emperor's grain have no conscience." They sing it as "I'd rather ride a cypress than a pine, I'd rather be a common surname than a collapse. Alas, alas, those who ride wolves have no wolf's heart." Unless one learns from a young age, it is not easy to be fluent and clear.

The Chantu people mainly rely on agriculture for their livelihood, followed by animal husbandry and commerce. Their food consists of wheat flour, yellow millet, millet, and rice. They often eat "jixi," which is made by mixing wheat flour with water and sticking it to the inner wall of a clay stove to be baked over a small fire. Feasts include "pilaf," "oily flatbread," "roasted meat," and "boiled mutton." Camels, horses, cattle, and sheep are all considered premium foods. Pilaf is made with half-cooked meat, topped with puffed rice, and seasoned with pepper, green onions, and lard. It is mixed well when cooked, served on a large platter, and eaten by hand, hence the name. Other dishes such as roasted meat and oily flatbread are also fragrant and delicious. These foods are also found in the interior, but the names and preparation methods are slightly different. The poor often eat "jixi" and drink water, willingly enduring hardship. The slaughter of livestock does not require an "ahong" (imam); it can be done by any member of the same faith. Pork is not eaten, nor is it raised. In counties such as Qiemo and Ruoqiang, pigs are almost extinct. In all the counties of southern Xinjiang, Han and Manchu people rarely eat pork in public, to avoid offending the Chantu people. Other items such as tea, sugar, grapes, dried apricots, and milk curd are used to treat guests. Smoking and drinking are forbidden by religious rules, but some still indulge occasionally. However, no one smokes opium, which is a very good thing. The Chantu people like three types of alcohol: one is brewed from sand dates, one is made from rice and wheat, with a light and sweet taste similar to Gansu's water wine, and the third is made by putting mare's milk in a leather bag, kneading it for a long time, and placing it in a warm place to ferment overnight. Xinjiang is rich in white grapes, which are crystal clear, seedless, sweet, and inexpensive, far superior to American beauty-brand raisins. If they could be expertly made into wine, it would surely surpass imported products.

Men wear right-fastening, narrow-sleeved, round-collared long gowns, with an unslit lower hem and a cloth belt around the waist, and a small knife is worn on the left. Summer clothes are plain white, while cotton and fur clothes vary in shades of red and brown. Ahongs and wealthy people wear a straight-front jacket over their long gown, resembling a Western-style coat. Women's clothes have collars but no fastenings. They cover their heads and wear a set of clothes underneath. Women who have given birth have an opening in the chest for breastfeeding. They prefer red and green colors and wear vests or short jackets (as shown in Figure 1). When going out, they cover their faces with a gauze scarf, holding it when the wind blows. If several men approach, they must stand aside to let them pass. The number of braids varies among women, all combed down the back. Their faces are painted with cosmetics, moderately applied. The eyebrows of young girls are painted together as one, to distinguish them from married women. They wear a flat-topped hat, embroidered with gold, silver, and colored threads, and flowers, which are quite expensive. Men's hats have a red tassel, or in winter they wear fur-trimmed cotton hats, and in summer they wear various styles of cloth caps. Men wear leather boots, reaching to the knees, while women also wear leather boots and shoes. Ahongs often wrap their heads in white cloth, greatly resembling the turbaned Indians, leading some to believe that this is the origin of the term "turbaned heads," but this is probably not the case.

Houses are flat-roofed and square, without ridges or gables, covered with mud bricks and decorated with floral patterns on the top. A skylight is opened for light and ventilation. The walls are carved with niches to store boxes, items, and bedding, arranged in an orderly manner, or covered with cloth curtains. A kang (heated platform) is built on the ground, slightly higher than a foot, hollow inside for heating in winter. Felt carpets are spread on top for sitting and sleeping. Farming families may pad wheat stalks under the felt to replace sun-drying. The kang is large and serves the same purpose as a wheat threshing floor in summer. Meals are eaten on a small table about a foot high for sitting around. Beds, tables, and benches are generally not provided. Stoves and cooking ranges are built along the edges of the wall, with pipes leading to the high roof to vent smoke. Turpan is hot in summer, requiring specially dug underground rooms.

Marriage age is mostly seventeen or eighteen for men and fourteen or fifteen for women. The old practice of marrying at thirteen is gradually decreasing. Marriage does not avoid blood relations, hence the saying, "Within three generations, uncles and brothers are respected; beyond three generations, there is no order." Some couples fall in love on their own, while others are introduced and presided over by parents, elders, ahongs, etc. Before the wedding, the groom's family sends gifts such as cattle, sheep, cloth, tea, and foreign wax to the bride's family and invites relatives and ahongs to the bride's home to discuss the marriage and recite scriptures to confirm the engagement. At the wedding, the bride is carried by her father or brother onto a horse and led to the groom's house with music. Distant relatives and neighbors offer food as congratulations and hold a banquet for a "weilang" (gathering). The groom and bride, in particular, have "weilang" rituals, and their every word and action is deliberately exaggerated by well-wishers for amusement, lasting a whole day before the crowd disperses. Divorce is called "linggan" or "yangdiao." The initiative is with the man, who must give the woman a generous gift. If the initiative is with the woman, she cannot take anything from the husband's house. Children are divided for upbringing, with ancestors guiding their education. After divorce, there are cases of reconciliation and restoration to the original state. Widows are allowed to remarry, and polygamy is permitted by custom. However, women must wait one hundred days after divorce before remarrying, probably due to physiological reasons. Whether it is a divorce or a marriage, an ahong is required to witness it. When a child is born, an ahong must recite scriptures and wash the child, and offer auspicious words. The child is named on the thirteenth day, with either two or three characters, or five or six characters, each with a meaning, but there are no surnames. Names are often the same, so the place of origin or occupation is prefixed to distinguish them. When a boy reaches the age of five or six, an ahong is invited to recite scriptures and remove the foreskin in a week. The same lighter procedure is performed by Han and Hui people in Gansu and Qinghai, which is said to be beneficial for physiological cleansing. Unfortunately, those who perform the circumcision often lack medical experience, easily causing bleeding and swelling in the circumcised children. Parents' inheritance is shared by children, usually seven tenths for sons and three tenths for daughters, or a ratio of two to one. When a woman marries, she can take what she receives to her husband's home, and it is returned to her in case of divorce.

The deceased is washed with water, wrapped in white cloth, and placed in a public wooden coffin, decorated with brocade. It is carried to the mosque, where the ahong recites the guiding scriptures, and then it is buried in the cemetery. A rectangular pit more than ten feet deep is dug, with a hole leading to the side from the bottom. The wooden coffin is removed, and the corpse is thrown into the hole. If it falls face down, it means the person committed a heavy sin and is imprisoned. Rapid chanting of scriptures is needed for redemption. If it falls face up, it means ascending to heaven, and rebirth in a blessed land is possible. If it falls sideways, it means a reduction of lifespan due to sin, and the soul is still wandering. Finally, the corpse is buried in the hole, facing west, and covered with earth to build a grave. The styles are different for men and women. Scriptures are recited on the third day to remove mourning clothes, and there are also several periods of mourning. In wealthy families, the corpse is kept in the central hall, and scriptures are recited for one or two days. However, the burial date is never delayed beyond the third day. The Hami royal tombs are walled with green glazed tiles, with a round top and square base, resembling palaces, covering many tombs below, truly magnificent architecture outside the pass (as shown in Figure 2).

"Weilang" is the name of the Chantu people's song and dance. The instruments include flat drums, sheng (mouth organ), and stringed instruments. The flat drum has a single surface with small iron rings attached inside. The left hand holds the edge, and the right hand strikes the drum surface, producing a "dong dong" sound, while the rings also make a "zheng zheng" sound. Combined with the blowing and plucking of the sheng and strings, the rhythm, fast or slow, high or low, all matches the emotions of the song and dance. The dance is performed either in a room or under the shade of trees. First, the opening drum lyrics are played, leading the male and female guests into the venue. The meaning of the lyrics is like, "Open a bright road, lead everyone to walk leisurely..." "There is a tree on the Gobi Desert, its shadow falls on the ground, there is a pedestrian on the road, his heart is on his sister." Then, the men and women dance in separate pairs, advancing and retreating in coordination, with neat steps. They raise their arms in gestures, and their waists and hips sway from side to side. Their expressions are serious, sad, and joyful, very vivid and lifelike. The scene is quite similar to Western dance, except that they do not embrace each other in pairs. After the social dance, they rest and dine together. Soon, the music resumes, followed by a dance to attract affection. The woman rolls a flower with a handkerchief and looks around at the male and female guests, choosing a loved one of the opposite sex and making a gesture of invitation and temptation. The invited person rises up and responds to the dance under the watchful eyes of the crowd, then exchanging an object with each other, and another person takes over. The state of children is moving. Generally, young girls like to invite young men, and women like to invite strong men. If the invited person does not respond, the inviter considers it a great insult. This custom probably originated in the nomadic era, when men and women pleased each other and flirted with flowers and plants, passed down to become today's custom. Finally, someone witty is publicly chosen to dress up as a madman searching for his wife, or a new bride escaping, etc., the rest of the entertainment is graphic and causes bursts of laughter before dispersing. Weilang borders on obscenity, and chieftains and ahongs often do not allow outsiders to visit. However, if it is believed that the inherent entertainment of the people is of poor taste, then social education should be actively promoted to improve the interests of the people's entertainment. If merely passive prohibition is used, it will be difficult to curb its natural development.

In addition, the Kazakhs mostly lead nomadic lives and rarely engage in agriculture. Although they share the same religion as the Chantu people, their culture is far inferior. The lives of the Mongols are roughly the same as those in Chahar and Suiyuan. The situation of the Gansu Hui people, except for religious beliefs, is mostly the same as the Han people. The Manchus are almost completely assimilated to the Han people.

Yutian Reorganization Takes Time

Authorities Have Drafted Steps, Starting with the Reorganization of Local Defense

Tianjin Correspondence: The Yutian Security Team, after much wrangling, finally completed its change of guard the other day. Zhou Yuying's troops carried out their entry into the county town and deployed troops to defend the Ya Hong Bridge. However, the departure of this security supplement team from Yutian was not what they wanted. If it hadn't been for the multiple meetings between the Chinese and Japanese sides, and the lack of any hindrance in diplomatic relations, Sun Yucheng, Liu Benzhi, and Feng Shoupeng's troops would never have willingly submitted to the transfer of defense. Although there was not much disturbance during the departure, the members of this team were a mixed bag, many of whom were unruly. Therefore, when Feng Shoupeng's troops marched east to Tangshan, and Liu Benzhi and Sun Yucheng's troops marched west to Tongxian, Yanjiao, and Xiadian, most of them deserted with their weapons along the way. Almost all of Feng Shoupeng's unit of plainclothes personnel, numbering two to three hundred, escaped. More than a hundred members of Shi Zhensheng's unit, the first company of the first battalion of Sun Yucheng's unit, also deserted. Wang Zixiu's unit, the second company, stopped advancing on the way to Yanjiao when they reached the border between Yutian and Tongxian. Because the Miting Bridge militia had assisted Wang Bingxiao's Yutian militia in attacking their unit, they took advantage of the passing of the large army and the militia's unpreparedness to launch a sudden attack, disarming the militia. More than a hundred merchants and residents were robbed. Li Yuansheng, the newly appointed commander of the Security Supplement Corps, could not enforce orders, and had no choice but to supervise the remaining troops to reach their defense areas first, and telegraph Yin Rugeng in Tianjin to request instructions. Feng Shoupeng's unit of plainclothes personnel initially fled to the border between Fengrun and Yutian counties, but after being pursued by the militia, they fled further out of Yanshan Pass. The Yutian-Jixian border had been harboring several hundred bandits from Liu Guitang's gang. Taking advantage of the Yutian team's change of guard, they attacked Linnancang and looted for two days and nights. After Zhou Yuying's troops assisted the militia in attacking, the bandits were overwhelmed and led by their leaders Wang Qingfang and Zhang Hanmin, suddenly fled out of Jieling Pass to join Feng Shoupeng's troops, waiting for an opportunity to strike. Zhou Yuying's troops, numbering only five hundred men in one battalion, had arrived in Yutian to maintain the county town and Ya Hong Bridge, and their strength was insufficient. Therefore, they did not dare to act rashly. The Reorganization Committee has been in contact with the Japanese side regarding what military actions to take against the various bandits and the rebel security teams and plans to increase the number of battalions by one, transferring them from Funing to assist. Once agreement is obtained, they can depart. Yin Rugeng came to Tianjin from Yutian on the 11th of this month and immediately contacted the Japanese military headquarters in Tianjin. A decision can only be made after Takahashi arrives. Yutian has been chaotic for more than a year, and the local area is almost completely empty. Small groups of bandits are rampant, and the local defense is domineering and does not listen to orders, and exceeds the number stipulated by the province by several times. Therefore, the authorities have decided to reorganize in steps, starting with the reorganization of the local defense, to ensure that all illegal organizations and militias are disbanded. Only then will they be reorganized according to the stipulated number. After this is completed, the next step is local reorganization, such as handling spring plowing relief and implementing rural cleanup. The rebel teams and bandits will then be gradually suppressed and pacified to allow those who have fled to return and those who have lost their jobs to find employment. It is planned to complete all these matters within two months. County Magistrate Zhao Congyi is currently discussing the progress with local people. However, the local vitality has been severely damaged. Although the plan is such, it will not be possible to pacify the area within half a year. (16th)

Relief: Fear of Material Shortages in Bandit Areas; Jiangxi Establishes a Trade Organization in Bandit Areas

Nanchang Correspondence: All the newly recovered bandit areas have undergone long-term occupation and destruction by the Red bandits, and the production mechanism and economic organization have been completely destroyed. The fear and difficulty of materials are self-evident. According to news from various front lines, Shicheng, Guangchang, Ruijin, Huichang, Yudu, Dian Country, Hengfeng, and Dexing, which were recovered last year, are all in ruins, with desolate sights everywhere. There is an extreme lack of able-bodied men, cash, and materials. Although they have been recovered for a long time, the local (bandit area) merchants are unable to resume business, and merchants from other places are hesitant to advance due to traffic difficulties and the desolate and unsettled local area. The disaster-stricken people after the robbery are extremely suffering from the lack of materials and high prices. The provincial government has specially decided to raise a large sum of tens of thousands of yuan to establish a trade organization in the bandit areas to transport and supply daily necessities to the bandit areas, and supply them to the disaster-stricken people in a cooperative manner, starting with the six counties of southern Jiangxi. According to political news, this organization will be co-located with the Rural Cooperative Association Office in Yudu and will first allocate 300,000 yuan to start controlling trade in the bandit areas. (March 14th)

Anhui Province Raises Funds to Relieve Spring Famine

Organizing Urgent Relief Works; Purchasing Seeds for Plowing

Anqing Correspondence: Anhui Province suffered a severe drought last year. The disaster-stricken area accounted for about two-thirds of the province's area. The direct and indirect losses of the people are almost incalculable. Now, during the spring season, the famine is even more pronounced. The provincial government recently planned to allocate 100,000 shi of relief rice and raise 160,000 yuan to select and organize urgent relief works, in order to appease the refugees and eliminate the source of bandits. The provincial government decided on this at a recent standing committee meeting. The Pi River, Chaohu Lake, Huayang River, Anjing, Qijing, and Li Huo road projects were approved for implementation. 1,700 shi of relief rice and 10,000 yuan of labor costs were allocated to the Pi River. 2,500 shi of relief rice and 50,000 yuan of labor costs were allocated to Chaohu Lake. 2,000 shi of relief rice and 300,000 yuan of labor costs were allocated to the Huayang River. 20,000 yuan has been allocated first, and the remaining 280,000 yuan will be allocated gradually after autumn. 2,200 shi of relief rice was allocated to the Anjing and Qijing roads, and 1,600 shi of relief rice was allocated to the Li Huo road. The relief rice will be allocated by the Food Regulation Committee. The labor costs for the Pi River, Chaohu Lake, and Huayang River will be raised by the Department of Finance and will be managed and distributed by the Department of Construction. The labor costs for the Anjing, Qijing, and Li Huo roads will be allocated separately. The entire Pi River and Chaohu Lake projects and the first phase of the Huayang River dredging project will be carried out to the extent that they can prevent summer floods. The Department of Construction will complete the allocated relief rice and labor costs for the Pi River and Chaohu Lake and the relief rice and 20,000 yuan allocated for the Huayang River within three months. The first phase of the Huayang River dam and culvert project will begin after the water level drops in autumn and will be completed in the spring of the 25th year with the additional 280,000 yuan. In addition, the provincial government previously approved the letter from the Provincial Disaster Relief Fund Raising Association, requesting to raise a large sum of money under the disaster relief preparation fund to check the situation of each county and distribute the purchase of seeds. It was issued to the Department of Civil Affairs and the Department of Construction for review. The two departments believe that the China Foreign Famine Relief Commission's special loan for agriculture in Anhui Province amounts to more than 800,000 yuan. According to the statistical report of the Anhui Provincial Rural Cooperative Committee, from the 21st year of the Republic of China to September of the 23rd year, the cooperative founded under the guidance of the committee in Anhui Province totaled 549, with loans of 250,218 yuan. Adding the agricultural loans for Huaining and other 15 counties this time, the estimated loan is 150,000 yuan, totaling no more than 400,218 yuan. The remaining amount is still less than 400,000 yuan. The seed problem for this year's spring plowing is extremely serious. Although the Department of Construction has drafted a notice to all places to follow and make overall plans in advance, and telegraphed the Executive Yuan to approve and allocate funds for purchasing and distributing seeds, it may not be effective in reality. Now, the provincial treasury is short of funds and cannot issue a large sum of money suddenly. The provincial government is requested to write to the National Economic Commission as soon as possible, ordering the China Foreign Famine Relief Commission to allocate the remaining special loan for agriculture in Anhui Province to the province for handling, or to the Anhui office of the commission to lend all the remaining funds to severely affected counties before the end of April, specifically for farmers to purchase seeds. (March 12th)

Farmers' Association and Chamber of Commerce Request Increased Tax on Imported Rice and Wheat

The Municipal Farmers' Association submitted a document to both the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "Regarding the dumping of foreign rice, which endangers the foundation of the nation, we earnestly request that you instruct relevant departments to prohibit it and increase the import tax rate to benefit agriculture. Our association has witnessed the large-scale import of foreign rice and wheat, which poses a deep and significant threat to the national economy and the people's livelihood. We have repeatedly petitioned your ministry to levy import taxes on foreign rice and wheat as a means of restriction. Your ministry graciously issued a decree on December 15th of the 21st year of the Republic of China, increasing the import tax rate on foreign rice and wheat. Farmers were hopeful for recovery, and rural revitalization seemed promising. Unexpectedly, last autumn, drought caused disaster, leading to poor harvests. Rice merchants from various regions rushed to Siam, Saigon, and other places to order large quantities of foreign rice to make up for the shortfall. Furthermore, after the United States implemented its silver policy, silver became expensive and gold cheap, causing exchange rates to fluctuate. As a result, the cost of foreign rice and wheat became low, leading to their dumping in China. According to a survey by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, over six million bags have been registered. The unregistered amounts reported by foreign firms are unknown. If increased taxes or other restrictive measures are not promptly implemented, the future of the rural economy and the people's food supply will be unimaginable. Moreover, the stock of domestically produced rice and wheat is still substantial in various regions. Even during the lean season, there is no need to worry. Our association is concerned that the already troubled financial situation will worsen with increased capital outflow, and the declining agricultural and commercial sectors will face further peril. Therefore, we dare to present the true situation and earnestly request your ministry to promptly instruct the relevant authorities to immediately adopt effective measures to prohibit rice merchants from placing further orders for foreign rice and to appropriately increase the originally set import tax rate on foreign rice and wheat to close loopholes and save the rural areas from imminent economic collapse. This is truly in the public interest."

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating: "To the Nanjing Ministry of Finance, we acknowledge receipt of a letter from the Municipal Grain Merchants Association on the 19th of this month (the original letter was published in this newspaper on the 16th). Based on this, we note that when your ministry issued an order last year to levy import taxes on foreign wheat, it was originally intended to collect at the highest tax rate. However, the current import tax on foreign wheat has not been fully collected, failing to curb the dumping of foreign wheat. With the domestic wheat supply abundant in various regions and the new wheat harvest about to begin, if the highest tax rate is not imposed, it will indeed harm the economic interests of farmers. Therefore, we report the situation by telegram and respectfully request your approval to increase the import tax on foreign wheat to close loopholes and protect domestic wheat. This is truly in the public interest. The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce bows, Hao Yin."

All-Zhejiang Association Concerned About Sericulture in Their Hometown

Letter: The All-Zhejiang Association requests advance funds for purchasing cocoons and raising prices. The letter, dated March 13th, was sent to the Silk Improvement (Control) Committee: "Regarding the matter, our Zhejiang has long been known for its sericulture. Since the frequent failures of silk cocoons in recent years, farmers have viewed silkworm rearing with trepidation. The sericulture industry is declining day by day. This year, following the early drought disaster, as the silkworm season approaches, we should plan ahead and take measures to rescue the industry so that the general silkworm farmers can benefit slightly, provide livelihood for the disaster areas, and promote the revival of farmers. The most urgent matters at present are to secure funds for purchasing cocoons in advance and to raise cocoon prices. The value of cocoons produced in Zhejiang reached a peak of 40 million yuan in the best years. Although production has decreased and prices have fallen, the total funds needed for purchasing cocoons in the province still amount to over 10 million yuan. Given the current stagnation of Shanghai's financial situation, the banking sector is mainly restricting loans. Furthermore, considering the bleak overseas silk sales and the dismal state of the domestic silk industry, it will not be easy to secure the large amount of cocoon loans as in the past. Therefore, whether the cocoon purchase is conducted by government or private entities, it is necessary to raise reliable large-scale funds in advance. Improvising at the last minute may lead to neglecting one aspect for another. If there is even a slight delay, the cocoon season will arrive, but the funds will not be fully secured, resulting in cocoons without a market, wasted seed and leaf capital, and the cocoons will turn into moths and pupae, becoming useless. If no remedial measures are taken, the benefits of sericulture in southeastern China will disappear. As for the purchase price of cocoons, it should be raised compared to the autumn cocoons of last year. Last year, the purchase price of autumn cocoons, after deducting the cost of seeds, was only about 14 cents per market catty. Silkworm farmers not only made no profit but also incurred losses. It is proposed that the cost of seed production be covered by the surplus from last year's autumn cocoons or by subsidies from the National Economic Council, and no longer deducted from the cocoon price. This would allow the price to be raised by 10 cents or more, so that farmers can earn some profit and be encouraged to raise silkworms. By securing a source of income, the industry can be preserved and not be cut off. Rescuing cocoon sales will benefit Zhejiang's production and alleviate the disastrous situation. Our association is concerned about the future of Zhejiang's cocoons and cannot remain silent. We hereby send this letter to your committee for your consideration and implementation. We eagerly await your response. Sincerely, The All-Zhejiang Association of Shanghai, to the Silk Improvement Committee and the Silk Control Committee."

Reply Letter: The Silk Control Committee replied on the 18th: "We have received your letter stating that this year, following the drought disaster, as the silkworm season approaches, we should plan ahead and take measures to rescue the industry so that the general silkworm farmers can benefit slightly, provide livelihood for the disaster areas, and promote the revival of farmers. The most urgent matters at present are to secure funds for purchasing cocoons in advance and to raise cocoon prices, and you have elaborated on the importance of these two aspects. We have taken note of your suggestions and appreciate your concern for the cocoon industry. However, the matter is important and requires detailed discussion. We will adopt and implement your suggestions to the best of our ability within the possible scope. We hereby reply and request your attention. (Remaining text omitted)."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Successfully Orders French Ship, Delivery on the Rhine River According to Contract

Xinsheng News Agency reports that Liu Hongsheng, the general manager of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, recognizing that domestic water and land transportation have been implemented successively, leading to an insufficient allocation of ships, purchased a large cargo ship from France. After approval by the Ministry of Transportation, negotiations were held with the French agent, and a contract has been signed, stipulating delivery on the Rhine River. The ship has a gross tonnage of 5,600 tons and a price of 7,750 pounds. At the beginning of the negotiations, this was equivalent to 150,000 Chinese yuan. Due to fluctuations in the exchange rate, the value was approximately 130,000 yuan when the contract was signed. Payment is divided into three installments. The first and second installments have already been paid. After signing the contract, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company sent a foreign captain from Shanghai to the Rhine River to take delivery of the ship. The captain has already inspected and is sailing the ship to Shanghai, expected to arrive by the end of next month. After arriving in Shanghai, the purchase price will be paid in full. The ship has already secured some cargo bound for Shanghai. After arriving in Shanghai, the ship will sail the Shanghai-Lianyungang route, specializing in transporting cargo connecting with the Longhai Railway, such as cotton. The ship was originally named Xiafei (transliteration). It has been decided to rename it, but the new name has not yet been determined.

Shipping Merchants Hold Meeting Today to Discuss Participating in Intermodal Transport; Private Ownership Attached to National Ownership Contradicts Original Intent

The Ministries of Transportation and Railways, due to foreign shipping companies demanding to participate in intermodal transport in our country based on the principles of open doors and equal opportunity, specifically summoned representatives of all shipping merchants in Shanghai to Beijing for a meeting. It has been decided to refuse this request. However, even for private shipping companies participating in intermodal transport, they must be affiliated with national companies and cannot establish separate joint offices to ensure that intermodal transport cargo is handled by state-owned vehicles, preventing foreign companies from exploiting loopholes. After arriving in Shanghai, the representatives of private shipping companies, recognizing that this matter has significant implications for the future of their businesses and contradicts the previous central government decision allowing private shipping companies to participate in intermodal transport, have decided to convene a meeting of representatives from all shipping companies at the Shipping Association at 2:00 PM today to discuss the major issue of changing the participation of private shipping companies in intermodal transport.
